***экспонат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экспонат.html>экспона́т</a> (9443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps borrowed from a Pseudo-Latin construction <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*expōnātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(something) exhibited, displayed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">expōnō</i> (the correct past passive participle is <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">expositus</i>).
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экспорт.html>э́кспорт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éksport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экспортный.html>э́кспортный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">éksportnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> export

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экстрасенс.html>экстрасе́нс</a> (18161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***электронный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a> (3875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электрон.html>электро́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elektrón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elektrónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> electron, electronic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> lámpa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron tube; vacuum tube</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>лу́ч</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnyj</b> lúč</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron beam</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:облако.html>о́блако</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnoje</b> óblako</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron cloud</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> púška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron gun</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нное</a></b> сродство́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnoje</b> srodstvó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron affinity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> teórija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron theory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:физика.html>фи́зика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> fízika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron physics</span></div></dd>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">электро-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elektro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электропередача.html>электропереда́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elektroperedáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электропередача.html>электропереда́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электропередача.html>электропереда́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электропередача.html>электропереда́ч</a></b>)
